consumer fetch request to record processing chain follows this flow in apache/kafka:\\n\\n**1. Fetch Request Building (Request Creation Phase):**\\nThe `FetchRequestManager.createFetchRequests()` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/FetchRequestManager.java:79) initiates the fetch request creation process. It calls `prepareFetchRequests()` to determine which partitions are fetchable and creates a Map of Nodes to FetchSessionHandler.FetchRequestData.\\n\\nThe `FetchRequest.Builder` class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/FetchRequest.java:153-200) constructs the actual fetch request with partition data. The builder is created in AbstractFetch.createFetchRequest() and configured with maxWaitMs, minBytes, isolation level, and maxBytes settings.\\n\\n**2. Sending Fetch Requests (Network Phase):**\\nThe `Fetcher.sendFetches()` method (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/Fetcher.java:105-120) prepares the fetch requests and sends them to brokers using `sendFetchesInternal()`. The `ConsumerNetworkClient.poll()` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/ConsumerNetworkClient.java:243-254) handles the actual network I/O, sending requests and receiving responses.\\n\\n**3. Response Parsing (Response Handling Phase):**\\nThe `FetchResponse` class (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/requests/FetchResponse.java:68-93) parses the broker's fetch response containing partition data and records. When the response arrives, `AbstractFetch.handleFetchSuccess()` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/AbstractFetch.java:150-248) processes it, creating `CompletedFetch` objects for each partition and adding them to the `FetchBuffer`.\\n\\n**4. Record Deserialization (Collection Phase):**\\nThe `FetchCollector.collectFetch()` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/FetchCollector.java:92-148) iterates through completed fetches in the buffer. It calls `initialize()` on uninitialized CompletedFetch objects, which extracts the MemoryRecords from the partition data. The `CompletedFetch.fetchRecords()` method (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/CompletedFetch.java) deserializes individual records using the configured deserializers.\\n\\n**5. Records Aggregation (Aggregation Phase):**\\nThe FetchCollector creates `Fetch` objects using `Fetch.forPartition()` (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/clients/consumer/internals/Fetch.java:43-54), aggregating deserialized ConsumerRecord objects grouped by TopicPartition.
